#You have avoided a phishing email Phishing emails can appear very convincing, and the attackers often use tactics to make them seem legitimate. Always verify the sender's email address, double-check the URL in any links, and never share sensitive information through email. In real-life situations, it's crucial to report suspicious emails to your organization's IT department or security team. However since you failed to report or alert your colleague about the email (b4r:"dotted")+(b4r-colour:red)[(text-colour:yellow)[''You have gained 2 points!!'']] <div> <img src="https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcShjjtvEn5QZNxWqETkAt_7YKzmvBOOQyJRsUAn5stq9LSHlgkeKEc7gkTqcQK13lEy2mg&usqp=CAU" </div> You are responsible for the company's data breech. Your boss is furious and sacked you immediately. Learning point: Phishing emails can appear very convincing, and the attackers often use tactics to make them seem legitimate. Always verify the sender's email address, double-check the URL in any links, and never share sensitive information through email. In real-life situations, it's crucial to report suspicious emails to your organization's IT department or security team. </div> </html> [[Ignore email]] [[Report email and alert colleagues]] #You have avoided a phishing email Phishing emails can appear very convincing, and the attackers often use tactics to make them seem legitimate. Always verify the sender's email address, double-check the URL in any links, and never share sensitive information through email. In real-life situations, it's crucial to report suspicious emails to your organization's IT department or security team.
